# Cooked Human Meat

# Description __

Salty meat from a human being, eating this will restore some hunger and health but reduces hydration. Maybe you should look for a better food source.

Page views: 2,409  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Raw Human Meat

# Description __

Raw human meat. Consuming will damage your health.

Page views: 3,258  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Snow Jacket

# Description __

A thick, high visibility Jacket. It will help keep you warm in any climate.

Page views: 2,638  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Jackhammer

# Description __

A Pneumatic Jackhammer to blast through ore nodes. The sheer power of this device requires no aiming as all weak spots will be instantly destroyed. Works well on human flesh. Can be refilled at a Workbench.

Page views: 9,440  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Jack O Lantern Angry

# Description __

A Lantern. Place it where you need light.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x2 Pumpkin



## Recycling Output __

  * x1 Pumpkin

# Jack O Lantern Happy

# Description __

A Lantern. Place it where you need light.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x2 Pumpkin



## Recycling Output __

  * x1 Pumpkin



Page views: 2,586  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Pickles

# Description __

Cucumbers in a vinegar bath, jarred by an amateur. Eat at your own risk.

# Kayak

# Description __

An improvised wooden kayak. Seats two players. Requires [paddle](/rust/paddle) to operate.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x250 Wood



## Recycling Output __

  * x125 Wood



Page views: 7,126  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Green Keycard

# Description __

A low level clearance card granting access to basic areas.

Page views: 3,851  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

#  [Rust Wiki](/rust/)

[Home](/rust/) / [Bone Knife](/rust/item/knife.bone)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/knife.bone)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/knife.bone~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/knife.bone~history)



# Bone Knife

# Description __

_Melee weapon crafted from bone fragments. Good for harvesting carcasses._   
  
  
  
  
  
  
  
  


# Infomation __

An early game weapon made out of bone. Very good to have early on due to it harvesting the most out of hunted animals (or humans!)

# Stats __

  * Damage **16**
  * Attack Rate: **86**
  * Atteck Size: **0.2**
  * Range: **1.5**
  * Flesh Gather: **10**



# Researching __

Can't be Research with any Work benches or The[Research Table](research.table) in the Game!

# Crafting __

  * **30x** [Bone Fragments](bone.fragments)



# Recycle __

  * **15x** [Bone Fragments](bone.fragments)



# Repair __

Can't be Repaired

# NPC Shop __

No NPC Shop Sell that item!

# Skins __

  * Yes

# Butcher Knife

# Description __

A sharp butcher knife. Extremely good at harvesting flesh from both dead or alive bodies.

Page views: 6,554  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Combat Knife

# Description __

Combat knife designed for close combat engagements, can attack while sprinting. Best in class at harvesting flesh.

Page views: 7,927  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/ladder.wooden.wall~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/ladder.wooden.wall~history)



# Wooden Ladder

# Description __

A ladder will help you climb walls in any base. Ladders can be placed in areas in which you do not have building privilege. They can also be picked up with a hammer if you do have building privilege.

Page views: 5,137  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __History](/rust/item/lantern~history)



# Lantern

# Description __

A Lantern. Place it where you need light, requires low grade fuel to work.

## Crafting Costs __

  * x25 Metal Fragments
  * x15 Low Grade Fuel



## Recycling Output __

  * x13 Metal Fragments
  * x8 Low Grade Fuel

Updated: A Long Time Ago

  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/largemedkit~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/largemedkit~history)



# Large Medkit

# Description __

A large medkit. If you get knocked down, carrying a large medkit in your toolbelt will guarantee you getting up 100% of the time.

# Obtaining __

Found in medical crates (50%), Locked crates (3%), elite crates (1%), military crates (1%), and oil rig scientists (0.1%).

# Usage __

Can be used as is, but is often recycled into [Medical Syringe](/rust/item/syringe.medical)

Healing |   
---|---  
Health | 0  
Healing | +100  
Hydration | 0  
Bleeding | -100  
Radiation | 0  
Poison | -10

# Description __

Leather from an animal. Used in many clothing items and more.

#  [Rust Wiki](/rust/)

[Home](/rust/) / [M249](/rust/item/lmg.m249)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/lmg.m249)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/lmg.m249~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/lmg.m249~history)



# M249

# Description __

High damage, high rate of fire, high range belt-fed light machine gun. Incredibly effective at range.

It can only be found in crates dropped by the Bradly APC or the attack helicopter.

  
  
  
  
  


# General Information __

With a high fire rate of 800 rounds per minute, the M249 can quickly mow down enemies at a distance. It can be loaded with 100 or 200 rounds of 5.56 ammunition, making it a formidable weapon against both players and structures.

Despite its power, the M249 has some drawbacks. It has high recoil and can be difficult to control, especially during sustained fire. It is also a heavy weapon, making it difficult to move quickly while carrying it.

## Attachment Compatibility __

* * *

The M249 is compatible with the following attachments:

  * Muzzle: 
    * Muzzle Brake
    * Silencer
    * Flash Hider
  * Sight: 
    * Holosight
    * 8x Zoom Scope
    * Simple Handmade Sight
    * 16x Zoom Scope
    * 4x Zoom Scope
    * 2x Zoom Scope
    * Laser Sight



## Damage __

* * *

The M249 deals 30 damage per hit to players and has a durability of 200.

## Interesting Facts __

* * *

  * The M249 is based on the real-life FN M249 SAW (Squad Automatic Weapon).
  * The M249 was added to Rust in the February 2018 update.
  * The M249 used to require a research table to craft, but it was changed to a crate-only drop in the April 2020 update.
  * The M249 is one of the most powerful and sought-after weapons in Rust, and it is often a key objective for players to obtain in order to gain an advantage in combat.

  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/lock.code~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/lock.code~history)



# Code Lock

# Description __

An electronic lock. Placed on boxes, doors and hatches. Locked and unlocked with four-digit code. Upon entry of the wrong code, you are shocked for 5 damage initially with damage ramping up for each consecutive wrong code.

Page views: 4,772  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

#  [Rust Wiki](/rust/)

[Home](/rust/) / [Key Lock](/rust/item/lock.key)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/lock.key)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/lock.key~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/lock.key~history)



# Key Lock

# Description __

Place on a door or a hatch to avoid any unwelcome guests. In order to activate the lock, you must aim at the lock and hold E to open the context menu. In the menu, hover your cursor over the 'Lock' option and click. After successfully locking, the green dot in the top right of the lock will change into a red dot and move to the top left.

Do not make a key! the person who places a key lock can open the door without a key. Crafting a key and carrying it with you allows anyone who kills you to open your door.

Page views: 5,537  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Locker

# Description __

A locker for keeping your clothes and armor safe!

## Crafting Costs __

  * x100 Metal Fragments
  * x50 Wood



## Recycling Output __

  * x50 Metal Fragments
  * x25 Wood

# Longsword

# Description __

A powerful 2-handed melee weapon with good range and high damage.

Page views: 6,187  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

#  [Rust Wiki](/rust/)

[Home](/rust/) / [Low Grade Fuel](/rust/item/lowgradefuel)

  * [ __View](/rust/item/lowgradefuel)
  * [ __Edit](/rust/item/lowgradefuel~edit)
  * [ __History](/rust/item/lowgradefuel~history)



# Low Grade Fuel

# Description __

Low Grade Fuel, used to power light sources, power boats and helicopters, and as fuel in Flame Turrets.

# Obtaining __

3 animal fat and 1 cloth is required to craft 4 low grade fuel.

[Crude Oil](/rust/item/crude.oil) can be smelted down in a [small Oil Refinery](/rust/item/small.oil.refinery) to produce 3 low grade fuel per crude oil.

Can be found in red barrels along roads and monuments.

Page views: 10,515  
Updated: A Long Time Ago

# Mace

# Description __

A powerful 2-handed melee weapon, It's unique design makes it easier to hit your target when compared to other more traditional weapons.

# Mace __

* * *

The Mace is a powerful two-handed melee weapon in Rust. Its unique design makes it easier to hit your target compared to other more traditional weapons.

## Description __

* * *

The Mace is made from a heavy metal head that is attached to a long wooden or metal shaft. The head is typically studded with sharp or blunt spikes, allowing it to deliver powerful, crushing blows to enemies.

Due to its weight and size, the Mace can be slower to swing than other melee weapons. However, it makes up for this with its raw power and the ability to stun or knock back enemies with its heavy blows.

The Mace is especially effective against armored enemies, as its blunt force can easily dent or damage armor plates. It can also be used to destroy structures and barricades, making it a useful tool for raiding enemy bases.

### Crafting Cost __

* * *

The Mace can be crafted at a level 1 workbench using the following materials:

  * 300 Metal Fragments
  * 20 Wood



### Damage and Durability __

* * *

The Mace deals 65 damage per hit to players and has a durability of 300.

Against structures, the Mace deals the following damage per hit:

Structure | Damage per hit | Hits to destroy  
---|---|---  
Twig | 4 | 8  
Wood | 3.2 | 11  
Stone | 2.5 | 14  
Sheet Metal | 2 | 19  
Armored | 1.5 | 26  
  
The Mace is a formidable weapon that excels in close-quarters combat and raiding. While it may not be the fastest weapon, its raw power and unique design make it a favorite among Rust players who prefer to take down their enemies with brute force.
